	<div class="term" id="md5-8f23331e498461261eacc5ff40824a91" about="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/AssignmentExpression">

  <h3 class="anchor" id="anchor1000008672"><span class="parrot-element-title parrot-class-title">Break Statement</span>

	  	  <span class="ti-menu active" style="border-radius: 10px;">Definition</span> 	  	      </span> 
  </h3>
  
  

      <p class="description">The BreakStatement class represents a break statement. The break statement has two forms: labeled and unlabeled. In case a break statement is labeled, the label is defined through the targetedLabel property</p>

  <h4>Definition</h4>

	<div class="term" id="md5-5eca038c55bd685b7481d41a97996933" about="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/ControlFlowStatement">


  <h3 class="anchor" id="anchor100843892"><span class="parrot-element-title parrot-class-title">Control Flow Statement</span>

			<span rel="rdf:type" href="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#Class">(OWL Class)</span> 
	
  	
  

    <span class="menu"> 
	  	  <span class="ti-menu active" style="border-radius: 10px;">Definition</span> 	  	      </span> 
  </h3>
  
  

      <p class="description">A control flow statement, that is a statement that regulates the order in which statements are executed.
Control Flow Statements break up the flow of execution by employing decision making, looping, or branching.</p>
    
  <div>
  
  
    <div class="ti" style="border-radius: 10px; display: block;"> 
  <h4>Definition</h4> 
			<p>The <strong>URI</strong> of this class is <span><code>http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/ControlFlowStatement</code></span></p>
		<hr>
	
		<table>
		  <tbody><tr>
	  <td>This class is a sub class of</td>
	  <td> 
	  	  <span class="parrot-element-ref parrot-class-ref" rel="rdfs:subClassOf" href="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/Statement">            	 <a href="#anchor1172997725">  Statement</a>
      </span>

	  </tr>
	
		  <tr>
	  <td>This class is a super class of</td>
	  <td> 	  
	  	  <span class="parrot-element-ref parrot-class-ref" rev="rdfs:subClassOf" href="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/BranchingStatement">            	 <a href="#anchor-669528449">  Branching Statement</a>
      </span>
	  	  <span class="parrot-element-ref parrot-class-ref" rev="rdfs:subClassOf" href="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/DecisionMakingStatement">            	 <a href="#anchor2072995254">  Decision Making Statement</a>
      </span>
	  	  <span class="parrot-element-ref parrot-class-ref" rev="rdfs:subClassOf" href="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/LoopStatement">            	 <a href="#anchor-330557287">  Loop Statement</a>

	<div class="term" id="md5-eec625afba416e9b24b834132949b15d" about="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/DecisionMakingStatement">


  <h3 class="anchor" id="anchor2072995254"><span class="parrot-element-title parrot-class-title">Decision Making Statement</span>

			<span rel="rdf:type" href="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#Class">(OWL Class)</span> 
	
  	
  

    <span class="menu"> 
	  	  <span class="ti-menu active" style="border-radius: 10px;">Definition</span> 	  	      </span> 
  </h3>
  
  

      <p class="description">A Decision Making Statement, that is a statement that break up the flow of execution by employing decision making. It can either be a if-then-else statement or a switch statement.</p>
    
  <div>
  
  
    <div class="ti" style="border-radius: 10px; display: block;"> 
  <h4>Definition</h4> 
			<p>The <strong>URI</strong> of this class is <span><code>http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/DecisionMakingStatement</code></span></p>

	<div class="term" id="md5-3782b13d13628baedac449c10dfa45a7" about="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/SynchronizedStatement">


  <h3 class="anchor" id="anchor1739708713"><span class="parrot-element-title parrot-class-title">Synchronized Statement</span>

			<span rel="rdf:type" href="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#Class">(OWL Class)</span> 
	
  	
  

    <span class="menu"> 
	  	  <span class="ti-menu active" style="border-radius: 10px;">Definition</span> 	  	      </span> 
  </h3>
  
  

      <p class="description">A synchronized statement, that is a statement that acquires a mutual-exclusion lock on behalf of the executiing-thread, executes a block, then release the lock.
In java it is of the form:
synchronized &lt;Expression&gt; &lt;Block&gt;</p>
    
  <div>
  
  
    <div class="ti" style="border-radius: 10px; display: block;"> 
  <h4>Definition</h4> 
			<p>The <strong>URI</strong> of this class is <span><code>http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/SynchronizedStatement</code></span></p>
		<hr>
	
		<table>
		  <tbody><tr>
	  <td>This class is a sub class of</td>
	  <td> 
	  	  <span class="parrot-element-ref parrot-class-ref" rel="rdfs:subClassOf" href="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/Statement">            	 <a href="#anchor1172997725">  Statement</a>
      </span>
	  	  </td>
	  </tr>
	
		
		
		  <tr>
	  <td>This class is a disjoint class of</td>
	  <td> 
	  	  <span class="parrot-element-ref parrot-class-ref" rel="owl:disjointWith" href="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/AssertStatement">            	 <a href="#anchor1046964855">  Assert Statement</a>
      </span>
	  	  <span class="parrot-element-ref parrot-class-ref" rel="owl:disjointWith" href="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/BlockStatement">            	 <a href="#anchor457351186">  Block Statement</a>

	  	  <span class="parrot-element-ref parrot-class-ref" rel="owl:disjointWith" href="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/ControlFlowStatement">            	 <a href="#anchor100843892">  Control Flow Statement</a>

	<div class="term" id="md5-1cacaeffe5db5e437a9b21d75355a1d9" about="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/declares">


  <h3 class="anchor" id="anchor1855345049"><span class="parrot-element-title parrot-property-title">declares</span> (Property)
  		  	
		<span rel="rdf:type" href="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#ObjectProperty"></span><img class="object-property-icon icon" src="CodeOntologyDoc_files/object-property-24.png" alt="object property">	
			
		   	
   	        <span rel="rdf:type" href="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#InverseFunctionalProperty"></span><img class="inverse-functional-property-icon icon" src="CodeOntologyDoc_files/inverse-functional-property.png" alt="inverse functional property">
    

    <span class="menu"> 
	  	  <span class="ti-menu active" style="border-radius: 10px;">Definition</span> 	  	      </span>   </h3>

  

      <p class="description">The declares property relates a code element to the elements it declares. For instance, a class is linked to its fields, methods and constructors.</p>
    
  <div>
  
  
    <div class="ti" style="border-radius: 10px; display: block;"> 
  <h4>Definition</h4> 

			<p>The <strong>URI</strong> of this property is <span><code>http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/declares</code></span></p>
	   
        	<p>This property is a  

    	    	    	    	<strong>inverse functional</strong>,      
    	    	    	    	    	    
    	    	    	<strong>object</strong> property.  
    	    	    	    	</p>

      </span></td>
      </tr>

      </tr>
     

    
          <tr>
             <td>The range of this property is</td>

	<div class="term" id="md5-1b143511bd0e9ede81ec0749d166f9d3" about="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/hasDimensions">


  <h3 class="anchor" id="anchor-1632246891"><span class="parrot-element-title parrot-property-title">dimensions</span> (Property)
  		  	
	<span rel="rdf:type" href="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#DatatypeProperty"></span><img class="datatype-property-icon icon" src="CodeOntologyDoc_files/datatype-property-24.png" alt="datatype property">		
			
		   	
   	    <span rel="rdf:type" href="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#FunctionalProperty"></span><img class="functional-property-icon icon" src="CodeOntologyDoc_files/functional-property.png" alt="functional property">    
    

    <span class="menu"> 
	  	  <span class="ti-menu active" style="border-radius: 10px;">Definition</span> 	  	      </span>   </h3>

  

      <p class="description">Links an array to the number of its dimensions. As an example, an array of type "int[][][]" has a dimensions count of 3</p>
    
  <div>
  
  
    <div class="ti" style="border-radius: 10px; display: block;"> 
  <h4>Definition</h4> 

			<p>The <strong>URI</strong> of this property is <span><code>http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/hasDimensions</code></span></p>
	   
        	<p>This property is a  

    	    	    	<strong>functional</strong>,      
    	    	    	    	    	    	    
    	    	<strong>data</strong> property.    
    	    	    	    	    	</p>
    	<hr>
    
        <table>
    
 
           <tbody><tr>
            <td>The domain of this property is</td>
      	  <td>
            <span class="parrot-element-ref parrot-class-ref" rel="rdfs:domain" href="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/ArrayType">            	 <a href="#anchor1833238049">  Array</a>
      </span>
      	  </td>
      </tr>
     

    
          <tr>
             <td>The range of this property is</td>
      	  <td>
            <span class="parrot-element-ref parrot-class-ref" rel="rdfs:range" href="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#int">              <a class="parrot-link" href="http://ontorule-project.eu/parrot/parrot?documentUri=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.w3.org%2F2001%2FXMLSchema%23int#anchor-1123686809">xsd:int</a>

	<div class="term" id="md5-d19c220e796abf42a8b8a5093b30846e" about="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/hasCanonicalName">


  <h3 class="anchor" id="anchor-536655499"><span class="parrot-element-title parrot-property-title">has canonical name</span> (Property)
  		  	
	<span rel="rdf:type" href="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#DatatypeProperty"></span><img class="datatype-property-icon icon" src="CodeOntologyDoc_files/datatype-property-24.png" alt="datatype property">		
			
		   	
   	        
    

    <span class="menu"> 
	  	  <span class="ti-menu active" style="border-radius: 10px;">Definition</span> 	  	      </span>   </h3>

  

      <p class="description">Links a class, enum or interface to its canonical name. For instance, the class Java.lang.String is linked to the string "java.lang.string"</p>
    
  <div>
  
  
    <div class="ti" style="border-radius: 10px; display: block;"> 
  <h4>Definition</h4> 

			<p>The <strong>URI</strong> of this property is <span><code>http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/hasCanonicalName</code></span></p>
	   
        	<p>This property is a  

    	    	    	    	    	    	    	    
    	    	<strong>data</strong> property.    
    	    	    	    	    	</p>
    	<hr>
    
        <table>
    
 
           <tbody><tr>
            <td>The domain of this property is</td>
      	  <td>
            <span class="parrot-element-ref parrot-class-ref" rel="rdfs:domain" href="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/ComplexType">            	 <a href="#anchor452785464">  Complex Type</a>
      </span>
      	  </td>
      </tr>
     

    
          <tr>
             <td>The range of this property is</td>
      	  <td>
            <span class="parrot-element-ref parrot-class-ref" rel="rdfs:range" href="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string">              <a class="parrot-link" href="http://ontorule-project.eu/parrot/parrot?documentUri=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.w3.org%2F2001%2FXMLSchema%23string#anchor-487667913">xsd:string</a>
      </span>
      	  </td>

	<div class="term" id="md5-7cdc03bc8aef0842abdf992847b3f050" about="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/isArrayOf">


  <h3 class="anchor" id="anchor-60043628"><span class="parrot-element-title parrot-property-title">is array of</span> (Property)
  		  	
		<span rel="rdf:type" href="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#ObjectProperty"></span><img class="object-property-icon icon" src="CodeOntologyDoc_files/object-property-24.png" alt="object property">	
			
		   	
   	        
    

    <span class="menu"> 
	  	  <span class="ti-menu active" style="border-radius: 10px;">Definition</span> 	  	      </span>   </h3>

  

      <p class="description">The isArrayOf property relates an arrray to the type of its elements at the finest grain. For instance, an array of type "int[][][]" is linked to the type "int". The number of dimensions of the array is specified by the dimensions property.</p>
    
  <div>
  
  
    <div class="ti" style="border-radius: 10px; display: block;"> 
  <h4>Definition</h4> 

			<p>The <strong>URI</strong> of this property is <span><code>http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/isArrayOf</code></span></p>
	   
        	<p>This property is a  

    	    	    	    	    	    	    	    
    	    	    	<strong>object</strong> property.  
    	    	    	    	</p>
    	<hr>
    
        <table>
    
 
           <tbody><tr>
            <td>The domain of this property is</td>
      	  <td>
            <span class="parrot-element-ref parrot-class-ref" rel="rdfs:domain" href="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/ArrayType">            	 <a href="#anchor1833238049">  Array</a>
      </span>
      	  </td>
      </tr>
     

    
          <tr>
             <td>The range of this property is</td>
      	  <td>
            <span class="parrot-element-ref parrot-class-ref" rel="rdfs:range" href="http://rdf.webofcode.org/woc/Type">            	 <a href="#anchor-1369297622">  Type</a>

		<span rel="rdf:type" href="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#ObjectProperty"></span><img class="object-property-icon icon" src="CodeOntologyDoc_files/object-property-24.png" alt="object property">

	})();
	/* ]]> */
  </script>
